Project Flamingo
Reliance Retail · Smart Bazaar, Gaya & Bodh Gaya · 2025 · 38-member team from 330 applicants

Overview

Project Flamingo was carried out to determine customer behaviour, operational effectiveness, trust drivers, and omnichannel preparedness in Reliance Smart Bazaar outlets in Gaya and Bodh Gaya. Part of a team of 38 selected from an applicant pool of 330, the project aimed at identifying obstacles to habitual shopping and JioMart adoption in a Tier-III market.

Research Methodology

  • Primary surveys: 400+ respondents across store locations
  • Ethnographic observations: real-time in-store behaviour, congestion, social dynamics
  • Store walkthroughs and process audits: layout, billing ops, inventory, fresh produce
  • Customer interviews and unstructured management interviews

Key Findings

  • Habit, trust, and convenience — not price — are the primary purchase drivers in Gaya
  • 84.7% customers feel secure; 49.1% say operational lapses significantly affect brand trust
  • 47% of customers rate billing experience as slow or worst during peak hours
  • JioMart: 36.6% never used the app despite digital nativity; ghost inventory and pricing inconsistency as key barriers

Strategic Recommendations

  • Express 5 billing counters for baskets under 5 items
  • Freshness Indicators in F&V section to match kirana trust cues
  • Scan and Go JioMart integration: Phase I-III roadmap
  • WhatsApp Order and Pick service for hyper-local 2km radius fulfilment
  • Staff-led JioMart onboarding and pricing transparency across channels

Presented To

Mr. Damodar Mal, CEO Reliance Retail, under guidance of Dr. Vinita S. Sahay, Director, IIM Bodh Gaya. CEO expressed appreciation for the team's thorough field-driven analysis.

📄 Open Full Report (Google Doc) 💼 LinkedIn Profile
Project RISHTA Impact Assessment
Tata Steel Foundation · Kalinganagar, Jajpur, Odisha · 2026

Overview

Impact assessment of Project RISHTA (Regional Initiative for Safe Sexual Health by Today's Adolescents), implemented across 39 Gram Panchayats in Danagadi and Sukinda blocks of Jajpur, Odisha. Addresses child marriage, teenage pregnancy, and adolescent reproductive health in tribal and mining communities.

Research Design

  • Mixed-methods: Stata 17 quantitative KPI analysis combined with qualitative field research
  • Multi-staged purposive sampling: 4 GPs (2 high prevalence, 2 low), 8 villages
  • In-depth interviews: Sarpanches, VLCPCs, ASHA workers, KND (adolescent couples)
  • FGDs: Saathiya peer educators, Youth Resource Club members

Quantitative Results

  • KND Training: Scores rose from 3.5/20 to 12/20 (t = -44.81, p<0.001)
  • Saathiya Training: Scores rose from 14/50 to 42/50 (t = -81.56, p<0.001)
  • Complete gender parity in knowledge gains — diverges from mainstream Indian SRH literature
  • 93.8% of counselled couples agreed to delay marriage post-counselling

Qualitative Themes

  • Active PRI leadership leads to near-zero child marriage in Ostapal and Uchabali GPs
  • Geographic isolation, infrastructural deprivation, and parental absenteeism as structural barriers
  • ASHA workers' credibility deficit in high-prevalence communities undermines counselling traction
  • Economic inequality structurally drives adolescent vulnerability

Strategic Recommendations

  • Coordinate with de-addiction services before counselling alcohol-prevalent households
  • Design targeted engagement activities for migrant parents (pre-migration counselling)
  • Institutionalise co-presence of PRI staff with VLCPCs during household visits
  • Establish seasonal touchpoints with migrant parents and appoint named adult guardians

WealthMax Product Audit
Bajaj Capital · Summer Internship · 2026

Overview

Independent product audit of WealthMax, Bajaj Capital's AI-powered portfolio analytics tool. Benchmarked against Dezerve across four dimensions: UX design, business model, analytics depth, and acquisition funnel architecture.

Scope of Audit

  • UX benchmarking: onboarding flow, dashboard design, information architecture vs Dezerve
  • Business model analysis: revenue structure, pricing, customer lifetime value considerations
  • Analytics depth: portfolio reporting, risk visualisation, AI recommendation quality
  • Acquisition funnel: lead capture, conversion touchpoints, digital marketing effectiveness

Portfolio Analysis

  • Live equity portfolio generating 16.97% CAGR
  • 115% cumulative excess returns over Nifty TRI benchmark
  • Consumer-first UX thinking applied to financial analytics presentation

Deliverables

  • 3 data-backed product improvement recommendations with implementation rationale
  • Structured presentation combining financial and UX analysis for senior stakeholders

    `; openModal('cert'); } // COMMUNITY ENDORSEMENTS — persistent via Google Sheets + Apps Script // ⚙️ SETUP: Paste your deployed Apps Script Web App URL below after following the instructions in SETUP_GUIDE.html const APPS_SCRIPT_URL = 'https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycby-lNj0AMVDTf9VD5C9NccV3jLisZ44JhvQV18PVeVgVlt34ujrN0mvDWwu0TzZ-nwdZw/exec'; async function loadEndorsements() { const list = document.getElementById('endorse-list'); const empty = document.getElementById('endorse-empty'); if (!APPS_SCRIPT_URL || APPS_SCRIPT_URL.includes('PASTE_YOUR')) { empty.textContent = '⚙️ Endorsements not yet connected. See setup guide.'; empty.style.display = 'block'; return; } empty.textContent = 'Loading endorsements…'; empty.style.display = 'block'; try { const res = await fetch(APPS_SCRIPT_URL + '?action=get'); const data = await res.json(); renderEndorse(data.endorsements || []); } catch(e) { empty.textContent = 'Could not load endorsements.'; empty.style.display = 'block'; } } async function submitEndorse() { const name = document.getElementById('e-name').value.trim(); const relation = document.getElementById('e-relation').value.trim(); const text = document.getElementById('e-text').value.trim(); if (!name || !text) { showEndorseMsg('Please enter your name and endorsement.', 'error'); return; } if (!APPS_SCRIPT_URL || APPS_SCRIPT_URL.includes('PASTE_YOUR')) { showEndorseMsg('⚙️ Endorsements backend not yet connected. See setup guide.', 'error'); return; } const btn = document.querySelector('.endorse-btn'); btn.textContent = 'Submitting…'; btn.disabled = true; try { const res = await fetch(APPS_SCRIPT_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain' }, body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'add', name, relation, text }) }); const data = await res.json(); if (data.status === 'ok') { document.getElementById('e-name').value = ''; document.getElementById('e-relation').value = ''; document.getElementById('e-text').value = ''; showEndorseMsg('Thank you! Your endorsement has been submitted.', 'ok'); loadEndorsements(); } else { showEndorseMsg('Something went wrong. Please try again.', 'error'); } } catch(e) { showEndorseMsg('Could not connect. Please try again.', 'error'); } btn.textContent = 'Submit Endorsement'; btn.disabled = false; } function showEndorseMsg(msg, type) { let el = document.getElementById('endorse-msg'); if (!el) { el = document.createElement('div'); el.id = 'endorse-msg'; el.style.cssText = 'font-family:var(--mono);font-size:0.7rem;padding:0.6rem 0.9rem;border-radius:5px;margin-top:0.6rem;'; document.querySelector('.endorse-btn').after(el); } el.textContent = msg; el.style.background = type === 'ok' ? 'rgba(26,82,204,0.12)' : 'rgba(200,50,50,0.12)'; el.style.color = type === 'ok' ? 'var(--accent3)' : '#e06060'; el.style.border = type === 'ok' ? '1px solid rgba(64,128,240,0.25)' : '1px solid rgba(200,50,50,0.25)'; setTimeout(() => { el.textContent = ''; el.style.background = 'none'; el.style.border = 'none'; }, 5000); } function renderEndorse(endorsements) { const list = document.getElementById('endorse-list'); const empty = document.getElementById('endorse-empty'); if (!endorsements || endorsements.length === 0) { empty.textContent = 'No endorsements yet. Be the first!'; empty.style.display = 'block'; list.innerHTML = ''; return; } empty.style.display = 'none'; list.innerHTML = endorsements.slice().reverse().map(e => `
    ${e.name || ''} ${e.relation || 'Peer'}${e.date ? ' · ' + e.date : ''}
    "${e.text || ''}"
    `).join(''); } window.addEventListener('load', loadEndorsements); // COUNTER ANIMATION function animateCount(el, target, suffix) { let current = 0; const step = target / 40; const timer = setInterval(() => { current += step; if (current >= target) { current = target; clearInterval(timer); } el.textContent = Math.floor(current) + (suffix || ''); }, 28); } const heroObs = new // LIGHTBOX function showImgLight(src, caption) { document.getElementById('lightbox-img').src = src; document.getElementById('lightbox-caption').textContent = caption || ''; document.getElementById('lightbox').classList.add('active'); document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; } function closeLightbox() { document.getElementById('lightbox').classList.remove('active'); document.body.style.overflow = ''; } document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closeLightbox(); }); // LAZY LOAD experience thumbnails function loadExpImages() { const tsfEl = document.getElementById('img-tsf'); if (tsfEl) tsfEl.src = IMG_TSF; const relEl = document.getElementById('img-reliance'); if (relEl) relEl.src = IMG_RELIANCE; const skyyEl = document.getElementById('img-skyy-cert'); if (skyyEl) skyyEl.src = IMG_SKYY_CERT; const skyyLorEl = document.getElementById('img-skyy-lor'); if (skyyLorEl) skyyLorEl.src = IMG_SKYY_LOR; const tedxEl = document.getElementById('img-tedx'); if (tedxEl) tedxEl.src = IMG_TEDX; // Cert card lazy images - load on hover document.querySelectorAll('.cert-lazy').forEach(img => { const src = img.getAttribute('data-src'); if (src) { try { img.src = eval(src); } catch(e) {} } }); } window.addEventListener('load', loadExpImages);
